Its melody, penned by the polymath Rabindranath Tagore, carries a solemn yet uplifting quality, reflecting the diverse cultural tapestry and aspirations of the nation. The song's structure is simple yet powerful, making it universally recognizable and deeply resonant across India.","trivia":["The song was originally composed in Bengali by Rabindranath Tagore as 'Bharoto Bhagyo Bidhata' and was first publicly sung on December 27, 1911, at the Calcutta Session of the Indian National Congress.","The full song consists of five stanzas, but only the first stanza was officially adopted as the National Anthem of India by the Constituent Assembly on January 24, 1950.","Rabindranath Tagore himself translated 'Jana Gana Mana' into English as 'The Morning Song of India' in 1919.","While often associated with the Bilawal raag, the anthem's melody is a unique creation by Tagore, blending traditional Indian musical elements with a Western-influenced harmonic It metaphorically equates the beloved's arrival to the blossoming of spring ('phool khilenge') and the arrival of a new dawn, signifying hope and renewal. The song's dramatic build-up and memorable chorus cemented its place in cinematic and musical history.","trivia":["Director James Cameron was initially against having a pop song over the end credits, preferring an instrumental score. Composer James Horner secretly worked with lyricist Will Jennings and Céline Dion to record a demo.","Céline Dion herself was initially hesitant to record the song, feeling she had already done too many movie themes. Her husband and manager, René Angélil, convinced her to record the demo.","The song won four Grammy Awards, including Record of the Year and Song of the Year, and an Academy Award for Best Original Song. It became one of the best-selling singles of all time, selling over 18 million copies worldwide.","The distinctive penny whistle (or tin whistle) motif that opens and recurs throughout the song was originally composed by James Horner for the film's instrumental score and later adapted into the song."],"musicxml":"musicxml/titanic-theme-song.musicxml"},{"id":"o-sanam","title":"O Sanam","export":true,"info":["Film/Artist: Lucky Ali","Scale: G BASS/MIDDLE"],"thumbnail":"images/o-sanam.jpg","background":"images/o-sanam.jpg","sections":[{"name":"STHAYI","lines":[{"lyrics":"","indian":"Hmmma: : : : : ."},{"lyrics":"","indian":"Pa: Ga ma Dha Pa ma: Ga Re"},{"lyrics":"","indian":"Re: Ma.
